[1] The beginning of an event
[2] Twenty-five years ago, specifically in August of Showa 19 (1944), in Japan, a pair of brothers were born. Due to being identical twins, the two boys looked incredibly similar, even to the point where their parents sometimes had difficulty distinguishing between them.
[3] The brothers had differences in their personalities. The older brother was introverted, calm, and well-planned, while the younger brother was enthusiastic and a doer. The differences in personality did not have any special significance, as over the course of twenty-five years, the brothers' lives were not influenced by their personalities.
[4] In Showa 19, it is unknown how many sets of twins were born in Japan, but it can be assumed that the brothers' lives were no different from those of other twin brothers. They all lived ordinary lives for twenty-five years.
[5] In August of Showa 19, Japan was in a dire situation on the battlefield, retreating continuously. The following year, Japan became a defeated nation. The impact of the difficult post-war life on the brothers' minds and bodies is difficult to describe in one sentence, but one thing needs to be mentioned. Soon after the war, their father died from malaria brought back from the battlefield, and from a young age, the brothers were raised solely by their mother. Therefore, despite their different personalities, both brothers deeply loved their mother.
[6] After turning twenty, the brothers pursued their separate paths in life, with different goals. Of course, this was not due to the common opposition and hatred between brothers.
[7] If they had continued to live according to their respective goals, perhaps their lives would have remained unknown to the world.
[8] However, one day, an event occurred.
[9] This event, which may seem trivial to the general public, had a catastrophic impact on the twin brothers and changed their attitudes towards society and life.
[10] Because of this event, the brothers, who had not seen each other for years, reunited and devised a plan together. They knew that this plan would be considered "evil" by society.
[11] "I don't care, I'm going to do it!" said the younger brother excitedly.
[12] The older brother, who was good at thinking, nodded firmly. "Let's do it!"
[13] "People in society are too despicable, so I want to take revenge!" the younger brother shouted.
[14] Although the older brother thought that the younger brother's use of the term "society" was too vague and inaccurate, he feared that the fire in his chest would be dispersed and weakened, so he did not comment on his brother's words.
[15] The plan was repeatedly refined and modified to ensure its success. The key to the plan's success was that the two brothers were twins, and their appearance could not be distinguished by others.
[16] To make the plan more perfect, they not only re-purchased identical clothes, hats, shoes, socks, and gloves, but also familiarized themselves with each other's habits as quickly as possible. After all, they had been separated for several years, and each had developed some unique language habits or action characteristics.
[17] The two brothers observed each other closely in the mirror.
[18] "So similar, this plan must succeed!" They both said confidently. Indeed, they looked so alike that it was impossible for them to look any more alike.
[19] The brothers divided their roles specifically. The younger brother was the main character in the plan, while the older brother played a supporting role. However, they were unsure who was at the greatest risk. Perhaps the older brother was in more danger.
[20] "If one person dies, the dead person bears all the responsibility. The other person can live on without a care." - The older brother said.
[21] "OK!" The younger brother nodded.
[22] A year later, all the preparations were completed, and in their opinion, the plan was flawless. The brothers began.

[60] After leaving the teahouse, the two of them watched a movie. When Jingzi got home, it was already past eleven o'clock. Her parents had gone to sleep, and she walked into the dining room to find a white envelope lying on the table.
[61] Koto sipped her tea while picking up the envelope and flipping it over. The letter was from "K Town Snow View Lodge" in Miyagi Prefecture. She had never heard of "Snow View Lodge" before, which was probably a hotel or a restaurant. Koto had never traveled to the northeast before. Anyway, her curiosity made her quickly open the envelope.
[62] When she opened the envelope, the first thing she saw was a colorful brochure. The cover was a colorful photo of a solitary two-story building floating in the vast, wave-tossed sea of snow.
[63] The photo was captioned: "This area is around 1,000 meters above sea level, with abundant snowfall, making it ideal for skiing trips." The brochure then introduced the "Snow View Lodge" itself. Koto thought, "Oh, that's the 'Snow View Lodge'." She sighed, thinking that even if the facilities were luxurious and the snowfall was abundant, she still couldn't go without paying. It was just an advertisement, and she had no connection to it.
[64] Later, she checked the envelope again and took out a note card. The note card had a few lines of text, and "Ms. Koto of the Ministry of Finance" was written by hand.
[65] Ms. Koto of the Ministry of Finance:
[66] In writing this letter, I am not considering the formality. Our hotel is celebrating its third anniversary, and we are offering free accommodation to a few residents of Tokyo to enjoy the snowy scenery of the country. The travel expenses, accommodation, and meals will be covered by our hotel.
[67] We hope that after your trip to the mountains, you will spread the word about our hotel when you return to Tokyo. Therefore, we would like to invite you to visit us.
[68] During the winter, the snow is very deep, and public transportation is suspended. After arriving at K Station, please call us, and we will send a snowmobile to pick you up from the northeast line K Station.
[69] The duration of the hospitality is from December 30th to January 3rd of the following year, a total of five days. We are making preparations to welcome you, and we sincerely hope that you will honor us with your presence.
[70] Enclosed is the round-trip ticket to K Station. Please use it.

[1452] The plan
[1453] But there's no need to panic. Continue to walk around town. There is a possibility that both of you will be arrested and taken to the police station. Stay calm and answer the questions during the trial. The more ambiguous the evidence, the better. It is estimated that you will be released that day. It will be very interesting to observe the expressions of the detectives and the victims during this time, and you can also taunt them. Note: During this period, the two brothers often wear the same clothes. Unify the testimony in advance.
[1454] First step
[1455] The brothers prepare the same clothes, and they can proceed. Since it's a trial run, you can choose a secluded small store. Even small stores, at the end of the year, have money. Pay attention, let the other party see your appearance freely. Do not leave any fingerprints, only fingerprints can distinguish the two of you, twins. Stay calm and do not panic. You will definitely win this battle.
[1456]    Second step
[1457]    Target large stores, especially department stores. Before that, it is best to attack another small store for practice. The method and precautions are the same as before. However, prior investigation is needed.
[1458]    Third step
[1459]    After robbing three stores, the police authorities will undoubtedly gather the victims to draw wanted posters. The wanted posters are undoubtedly very similar to your own appearance.
[1460]    Fourth step
[1461] At this point, you should have gained confidence. Confidence makes people feel at ease and helps success. However, confidence can also make people careless. Therefore, extra caution is required. However, as long as you are not caught at the scene of the crime and do not leave fingerprints, you are absolutely safe. At this time, you need to pay attention to the police's movements. The police authorities know the criminal's surname and address, but cannot arrest them. This is unprecedented for them. Police have always thought they are superior to others and are not to be touched, so they must be angry and frustrated. However, the police can only track and monitor you. When you go out, you must remember that someone is tailing you. Shaking off the tail is easy. Going to a crowded movie theater can help you escape surveillance. Alternatively, you can turn around and catch the police who are following you, make fun of them, and they will be embarrassed and in trouble, which will be a great pleasure. After escaping surveillance, go to the target of the robbery. During the New Year period, there is a lot of money on the streets. Movie theaters, amusement parks, etc. are all suitable prey. However, when the robbery occurs, the police will certainly monitor your apartment and wait for you to return. If the money is carried with you, it will become evidence and you will be arrested. The gun can still be hidden behind a trash can or sealed in a nylon bag and sunk in a pond. What about the money? Prepare a sturdy large envelope in advance, put the money in it, and then put it in the mailbox on the way. Stick enough stamps to avoid insufficient postage and trouble with the post office. If the postman has evil intentions and steals the money for himself, it is unnecessary to worry. The postman will not announce that he has done something wrong.
[1462] Fifth Step
[1463] Even after the successful robbery and the money has been mailed, there are still problems. Although the stupid police will never think that you used the mailing trick. However, they are monitoring your apartment day and night. To ensure the safe delivery of the mail to your apartment, you can adopt a diversionary tactic to lure the police away from your apartment. On the day before the robbery, store a handbag full of old books in the station near the scene of the crime. The next day, the two of you go together to pick it up. The police will certainly think they have succeeded and check its contents. You can take advantage of this opportunity to make fun of this bunch of incompetents. Meanwhile, the mail will safely arrive at your apartment.
[1464] Sixth Step
[1465] At this stage, you should pay attention to the dynamics of the media. The strange situation of the police authorities knowing the criminals but unable to arrest them will not be ignored by the gossiping press. Of course, they dare not publish your names. If they dare to name and shame, you can sue them for defamation and get a compensation of hundreds of millions of yen. So the media itself is not scary. What is scary is that the media will put pressure on the police, and the police will be angry and frustrated. The police will not dare to do anything to you, but they will only try to make you change your appearance so that they can distinguish you. Although they dare not force you, you can ignore them, but it is best to agree. For example, agree that the younger brother will wear a leather jacket when he goes out. The police will be confused. You can take advantage of the police's carelessness and commit a new robbery that day. Wear the leather jacket when committing the robbery. The police will certainly come to arrest the younger brother when they hear the case report. At this time, the two brothers can stage a farce and accuse each other of wearing the leather jacket to commit the crime. The police will still be unable to arrest you.
[1466]    Notes. One, do not get caught on the scene. When the police come to the apartment, it is best for the two of you to undress and go to sleep, in order to act. In order to have enough time, after stealing the money, tie and gag the other party so that they cannot report within an hour. Two, the stolen money should not be carried home, and it is safest for the police to enter your residence with no money. When the police see that you have no money, they will certainly pay attention to the mail, because you have successfully used this method before. Taking advantage of the police's stupid judgment, you will have a lot of fun playing them again. There are many ways to play the police, and here is just one example: the two of you argue endlessly, and the younger brother takes the opportunity to leave and move to a hotel that has been reserved in advance. The police will certainly suspect that there is something fishy. The next day, the younger brother receives a letter at the hotel. What will the police think? Perhaps even a three-year-old child could guess it. The police will certainly force the younger brother to open the letter in front of them and check if there is money inside. The younger brother should pretend to be difficult, pour oil on the fire, make the police impatient, eager, and angry. If the size and thickness of the envelope are similar to that of money, the police will be more determined. Whatever is inside the envelope is suitable, but naked photos are the most suitable, as they can be used as an excuse that it cannot be shown to outsiders. When the police see that it is a naked photo, the scene will be very exciting. The police will definitely make another mistake in judgment and lose confidence in their suspicion of the letter. Then, what should be done with the stolen money? - The letter ends here. Below is written in red: "To know what happens next, please wait for the next episode."

[1825] Tenth stage
[1826] 2:57 PM.
